                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                            etype 0x8848
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 666 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8848/MPLS multicast/Multicast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                            etype 0x8848
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 699 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8848/MPLS multicast/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            etype 0x8848
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 733 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8863/PPPoE Discovery/PADI/Broadcast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                            etype 0x8863
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 766 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8863/PPPoE Discovery/----/Multicast"

                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                            etype 0x8863
                        exit
                    exit

                    exit
